#A unique sample identifier.	Identifier to uniquely specify a patient.	The main cancer type as defined by the Oncotree cancer classification system for precision oncology	The type assigned to a sample (i.e., normal, primary, met, recurrence)	The gene panel or assay used used to perform targeted NGS on the sample	Sequencing coverage	Proportion of cancer cells in tumor sample	The assigned Oncotree code of the sample as defined by the Oncotree cancer classification system for precision oncology.	Microsatellite Instability (MSI) score 	Directly related to MSI Score; Possible values include Stable, Instable, Indeterminate, or Do not report	Indicates if there exists a matched normal used for tumor sample analysis	TMB (nonsynonymous)	Cancer Type Detailed
